listcategories 	  -	 show a list of categories. 
listall 	  -	 show a list of all records. 
createdatabase 	  -	 create database. 
help\h 	  -	 show a list of commands. 
exit 	  -	 exit the system. 
start 	  -	 start a new window to run commands. 
version 	  -	 display the app version. 
connections 	  -	 show datastores connection states.
